STATUTORY INSTRUMENTS
2024 No. 321
VETERINARY SURGEONS
The Veterinary Surgeons and Veterinary Practitioners (Registration) (Amendment) Regulations Order of Council 2024
Made
6th March 2024
Coming into force
1st April 2024
At the Council Chamber, Whitehall, the 6th day of March 2024
By the Lords of His Majesty’s Most Honourable Privy Council
The Council of the Royal College of Veterinary Surgeons has made the Veterinary Surgeons and Veterinary Practitioners (Registration) (Amendment) Regulations 2023 (“the Regulations”), which are set out in the Schedule to this Order, in exercise of powers conferred by section 11 of the Veterinary Surgeons Act 1966(1) (“the Act”).
By virtue of section 25(1) of the Act, the Regulations do not have effect unless approved by order of the Privy Council.
Their Lordships make this Order in exercise of the powers conferred by section 25(1) and (2) of the Act.
(1)
1966 c. 36; section 11(7) was inserted by S.I. 2008/1824 and was repealed by S.I. 2019/454.Citation and commencement
1.  This Order may be cited as the Veterinary Surgeons and Veterinary Practitioners (Registration) (Amendment) Regulations Order of Council 2024 and comes into force on 1st April 2024.Approval
2.  The Veterinary Surgeons and Veterinary Practitioners (Registration) (Amendment) Regulations 2023 set out in the Schedule are approved.Revocation
3.  The Veterinary Surgeons and Veterinary Practitioners (Registration) (Amendment) Regulations Order of Council 2023(1) is revoked.
(1)
S.I. 2023/242.Richard Tilbrook
Clerk of the Privy CouncilArticle 2
SCHEDULE
The Veterinary Surgeons and Veterinary Practitioners (Registration) (Amendment) Regulations 2023
The Council of the Royal College of Veterinary Surgeons, in exercise of its powers under section 11 of the Veterinary Surgeons Act 1966, makes the following Regulations.
For Part 4 (Fees payable) of the Veterinary Surgeons and Veterinary Practitioners (Registration) Regulations 2014(1), substitute—
“PART 4
Fees payable
Table 1
Registration fees payable under regulation 9
Type of registrant Fee payable (£)
New graduates registered by 31 December following graduation 200
Other persons registered between 1 April and 30 September 402
Other persons registered between 1 October and 31 March 200
Table 2
Fees for temporary registrants payable under regulations 10, 11 and 14
Type of fee Fee payable (£)
Normal registration fee 402
Registration fee for practice restricted to period of six months or less 200
Retention fee 402
Table 3
Retention fees payable under regulation 15
Circumstances Column A – Fee payable if payment received on or before 30 April (£) Column B – Fee payable if payment received after 30 April (£)
Standard registrant 402 437
Overseas practising registrant 200 235
Non-practising registrant 66 101
Table 4
Additional fees payable under regulations 16 and 17
Fee paid (£) New circumstance
Extra sum payable if change takes place before 1 October
(£)
Extra sum payable if change takes place on or after 1 October
(£)
66 or 101 Practising, but not in the British Islands 134 67
66 or 101 Practising in the British Islands 336 168
200 or 235 Practising in the British Islands 202 101
Table 5
Credits payable under regulation 18
Fee paid (£) New circumstance Sum to be credited (£)
402 or 437 Non-practising registrant 168
402 or 437 Overseas practising registrant 101
200 or 235 Non-practising registrant 67
Table 6
Restoration fees payable under regulation 19
Type of restoration Fee payable (£)
Restoration under section 11(3) of the Act following removal for non-receipt of retention fee 402
Restoration in other circumstances 124”
(1)
S.I. 2014/3493, amended by S.I. 2023/242.Richard Tilbrook
Clerk of the Privy CouncilArticle 2

For Part 4 (Fees payable) of the Veterinary Surgeons and Veterinary Practitioners (Registration) Regulations 2014(1), substitute—
“PART 4
Fees payable
Table 1
Registration fees payable under regulation 9
Type of registrant Fee payable (£)
New graduates registered by 31 December following graduation 200
Other persons registered between 1 April and 30 September 402
Other persons registered between 1 October and 31 March 200
Table 2
Fees for temporary registrants payable under regulations 10, 11 and 14
Type of fee Fee payable (£)
Normal registration fee 402
Registration fee for practice restricted to period of six months or less 200
Retention fee 402
Table 3
Retention fees payable under regulation 15
Circumstances Column A – Fee payable if payment received on or before 30 April (£) Column B – Fee payable if payment received after 30 April (£)
Standard registrant 402 437
Overseas practising registrant 200 235
Non-practising registrant 66 101
Table 4
Additional fees payable under regulations 16 and 17
Fee paid (£) New circumstance
Extra sum payable if change takes place before 1 October
(£)
Extra sum payable if change takes place on or after 1 October
(£)
66 or 101 Practising, but not in the British Islands 134 67
66 or 101 Practising in the British Islands 336 168
200 or 235 Practising in the British Islands 202 101
Table 5
Credits payable under regulation 18
Fee paid (£) New circumstance Sum to be credited (£)
402 or 437 Non-practising registrant 168
402 or 437 Overseas practising registrant 101
200 or 235 Non-practising registrant 67
Table 6
Restoration fees payable under regulation 19
Type of restoration Fee payable (£)
Restoration under section 11(3) of the Act following removal for non-receipt of retention fee 402
Restoration in other circumstances 124”
(1)
S.I. 2014/3493, amended by S.I. 2023/242.Richard Tilbrook
Clerk of the Privy CouncilArticle 2

The Veterinary Surgeons and Veterinary Practitioners (Registration) (Amendment) Regulations 2023
The Council of the Royal College of Veterinary Surgeons, in exercise of its powers under section 11 of the Veterinary Surgeons Act 1966, makes the following Regulations.
For Part 4 (Fees payable) of the Veterinary Surgeons and Veterinary Practitioners (Registration) Regulations 2014(1), substitute—
“PART 4
Fees payable
Table 1
Registration fees payable under regulation 9
Type of registrant Fee payable (£)
New graduates registered by 31 December following graduation 200
Other persons registered between 1 April and 30 September 402
Other persons registered between 1 October and 31 March 200
Table 2
Fees for temporary registrants payable under regulations 10, 11 and 14
Type of fee Fee payable (£)
Normal registration fee 402
Registration fee for practice restricted to period of six months or less 200
Retention fee 402
Table 3
Retention fees payable under regulation 15
Circumstances Column A – Fee payable if payment received on or before 30 April (£) Column B – Fee payable if payment received after 30 April (£)
Standard registrant 402 437
Overseas practising registrant 200 235
Non-practising registrant 66 101
Table 4
Additional fees payable under regulations 16 and 17
Fee paid (£) New circumstance
Extra sum payable if change takes place before 1 October
(£)
Extra sum payable if change takes place on or after 1 October
(£)
66 or 101 Practising, but not in the British Islands 134 67
66 or 101 Practising in the British Islands 336 168
200 or 235 Practising in the British Islands 202 101
Table 5
Credits payable under regulation 18
Fee paid (£) New circumstance Sum to be credited (£)
402 or 437 Non-practising registrant 168
402 or 437 Overseas practising registrant 101
200 or 235 Non-practising registrant 67
Table 6
Restoration fees payable under regulation 19
Type of restoration Fee payable (£)
Restoration under section 11(3) of the Act following removal for non-receipt of retention fee 402
Restoration in other circumstances 124”
(1)
S.I. 2014/3493, amended by S.I. 2023/242.Richard Tilbrook
